(product.ID=SaleProductPriceDisplay.PRODUCT_ID) LEFT JOIN `sale` `SalePriceDisplay` ON (SaleProductPriceDisplay.SALE_ID=SalePriceDisplay.ID AND `SalePriceDisplay`.`active` = 1) WHERE (NOT ISNULL(`requested_locale_i18n`.ID) OR NOT ISNULL(`default_locale_i18n`.ID)) AND CategorySelect.CATEGORY_ID IN ('16') AND product.VISIBLE=1 GROUP BY product.ID ORDER BY i18n_TITLE ASC LIMIT 8
